if not game.IsLoaded then
    game.Loaded:Wait()
end
if getgenv().QuantumOnyx then
    print("Already Executed")
    return
end
getgenv().QuantumOnyx = true
local a = game:GetService("Workspace")
local b = game:GetService("Players")
local c = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
local d = game:GetService("CollectionService")
local e = game:GetService("RunService")
local f = game:GetService("Lighting")
local g = game:GetService("TeleportService")
local h = game:GetService("HttpService")
local i = game:GetService("CoreGui")
local j = b.LocalPlayer
local k = c:WaitForChild("Remotes")
local l = k:WaitForChild("CommF_")
local m = j:WaitForChild("Data"):WaitForChild("Level")
local n = a:WaitForChild("Enemies")
local o = a:WaitForChild("Map")
local p = a:WaitForChild("_WorldOrigin")
local q = c:WaitForChild("Modules")
local r = q:WaitForChild("Net")
local s = require(c:WaitForChild("GuideModule"))
local t =
    loadstring(
    game:HttpGet("https://raw.githubusercontent.com/flazhy/QuantumOnyx/refs/heads/main/Util/BloxFruitModule/Loops.lua")
)()
local u =
    loadstring(
    game:HttpGet("https://raw.githubusercontent.com/flazhy/QuantumOnyx/refs/heads/main/Util/BloxFruitModule/Quests.lua")
)()
local v =
    loadstring(game:HttpGet("https://raw.githubusercontent.com/flazhy/QuantumOnyx/refs/heads/main/Util/Library.lua"))()
local w = {}
local x = game.PlaceId
local y = x == 2753915549 or x == 85211729168715
local z = x == 4442272183 or x == 79091703265657
local A = x == 7449423635 or x == 100117331123089
local function B(C, D, E)
    v.Notification:Notify({Title = C, Description = D}, {Time = E or 5})
end
function FireInvoke(...)
    return l:InvokeServer(...)
end
local function F()
    local G = j.Character
    if G and G.Parent then
        return G
    end
    return j.CharacterAdded:Wait()
end
local function H(G)
    G = G or F()
    return G:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") or G:WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart", 5)
end
local function I(J)
    local K = J.Position
    local L, M = math.huge, nil
    local N = {
        Sea_1 = {
            Vector3.new(-7894.62, 5545.49, -380.25),
            Vector3.new(-4607.82, 872.54, -1667.56),
            Vector3.new(61163.85, 11.76, 1819.78),
            Vector3.new(3876.28, 35.11, -1939.32)
        },
        Sea_2 = {
            Vector3.new(-288.46, 306.13, 598),
            Vector3.new(2284.91, 15.15, 905.48),
            Vector3.new(923.21, 126.98, 32852.83),
            Vector3.new(-6508.56, 89.03, -132.84)
        },
        Sea_3 = {
            Vector3.new(-5058.77, 314.52, -3155.88),
            Vector3.new(5756.84, 610.42, -253.93),
            Vector3.new(-12463.87, 374.91, -7523.77),
            Vector3.new(28282.57, 14896.85, 105.1),
            Vector3.new(5661.5322265625, 1013.0907592773438, -334.9649963378906),
            Vector3.new(5319, 23, -93),
            Vector3.new(5651, 1018, -350),
            Vector3.new(28286, 14897, 103)
        }
    }
    local O = y and N.Sea_1 or z and N.Sea_2 or A and N.Sea_3 or {}
    for P, Q in ipairs(O) do
        local R = (Q - K).Magnitude
        if R < L then
            L, M = R, Q
        end
    end
    local S = H().Position
    return L <= (K - S).Magnitude and M or nil
end
local function T(U)
    FireInvoke("requestEntrance", U)
    local V = H()
    V.CFrame = V.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 40, 0)
    task.wait(0.5)
end
local W = false
local X = 0
local Y = 5
local Z = nil
local _ = nil
local function a0(a1)
    W = false
    if Z then
        return
    end
    Z = true
    local V = H()
    if not V or not V.Parent then
        Z = nil
        return
    end
    local a2 = V.Parent:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
    if not a2 then
        Z = nil
        return
    end
    local a3 = typeof(a1) == "Vector3" and CFrame.new(a1) or a1
    if not a3 then
        Z = nil
        return
    end
    if _ then
        _:Disconnect()
        _ = nil
    end
    local a4 = {Stop = false, MinInterval = 0, LastUpdate = 0, CurrentCF = nil}
    function a4:SetCF(a5)
        local a6 = tick()
        if a6 - self.LastUpdate >= self.MinInterval then
            self.LastUpdate = a6
            V.CFrame = a5
        end
        self.CurrentCF = a5
    end
    _ =
        V:GetPropertyChangedSignal("Parent"):Connect(
        function()
            if W or a4.Stop or j.Character.Humanoid.Health <= 0 then
                if _ then
                    _:Disconnect()
                    _ = nil
                end
                return
            end
            if a4.CurrentCF then
                V.CFrame = a4.CurrentCFq
            end
        end
    )
    local function a7(a8, a9)
        local aa = (a9.Position - a8.Position).Magnitude
        if aa == 0 then
            Z = nil
            if _ then
                _:Disconnect()
                _ = nil
            end
            return
        end
        local ab = 0
        while true do
            if W or a4.Stop or a2.Health <= 0 then
                Z = nil
                if _ then
                    _:Disconnect()
                    _ = nil
                end
                return
            end
            local ac = tonumber(w.TweenSpeed) or 250
            if ac < 0.1 then
                ac = 0.1
            end
            local ad = task.wait()
            ab = ab + ac * ad
            local ae = math.clamp(ab / aa, 0, 1)
            local af = a8:Lerp(a9, ae)
            a4:SetCF(af)
            local ag = (a9.Position - V.Position).Magnitude
            if ag <= 20 or ae >= 1 then
                a4.Stop = true
                a4:SetCF(a9)
                Z = nil
                if _ then
                    _:Disconnect()
                    _ = nil
                end
                return
            end
        end
    end
    local ah = I(a3)
    if ah and tick() - X >= Y then
        T(ah)
        X = tick()
        task.wait(0.1)
    end
    a7(V.CFrame, a3)
end
local function ai(aj, ak)
    W = false
    a0(typeof(aj) == "Vector3" and CFrame.new(aj) or aj)
    if W then
        StopTween()
        return
    end
    if ak then
        EnableNoclip()
        DisableCollisions()
    else
        local V = H()
        if V then
            local al = V:FindFirstChild("PartVelocuty")
            if al then
                al:Destroy()
            end
        end
    end
end
function StopTween()
    W = true
    Z = nil
    NoclipBody = nil
    if _ then
        _:Disconnect()
        _ = nil
    end
    local V = H()
    if V then
        local am = V:FindFirstChild("PartVelocuty")
        if am then
            am:Destroy()
        end
    end
end
local NoclipBody = nil
function EnableNoclip()
    if not j.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart"):FindFirstChild("PartVelocuty") then
        if NoclipBody then
            NoclipBody:Destroy()
        end
        NoclipBody = Instance.new("BodyVelocity", j.Character.HumanoidRootPart)
        NoclipBody.Name = "PartVelocuty"
        NoclipBody.MaxForce = Vector3.new(4e4, 4e4, 4e4)
        NoclipBody.Velocity = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)
        NoclipBody.P = 1250
    end
end
function DisableCollisions()
    local an = j.Character
    for P, ao in next, an:GetChildren() do
        if ao:IsA("BasePart") and ao.CanCollide then
            ao.CanCollide = false
        end
    end
end
local ap = 1
task.spawn(
    function()
        while true do
            ap = 1
            if ap == 1 then
                Pos = Vector3.new(0, PosY, 0)
            end
            task.wait(0.1)
        end
    end
)
